<p>A <b>grass block</b> is a natural <a href="/w/Block" title="Block">block</a> that generates abundantly across the surface of the <a href="/w/Overworld" title="Overworld">Overworld</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Obtaining">Obtaining</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=1&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Obtaining">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Obtaining">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Breaking">Breaking</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=2&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Breaking">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Breaking">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A grass block can be obtained by mining it using a <a href="/w/Tool" title="Tool">tool</a> enchanted with <a href="/w/Silk_Touch" title="Silk Touch">Silk Touch</a>. Otherwise, it drops <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a>. It can also be obtained by killing an <a href="/w/Enderman" title="Enderman">enderman</a> that is holding a grass block.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Natural_generation">Natural generation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=3&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Natural generation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Natural generation">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Grass blocks generate naturally in most <a href="/w/Biome" title="Biome">biomes</a> in the <a href="/w/Overworld" title="Overworld">Overworld</a>, and as part of <a href="/w/Village" title="Village">villages</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Ancient_cities" title="Ancient cities">ancient cities</a>.
</p>
<div class="mcw-calc" data-block-names="Grass Block" data-blocks="minecraft:grass_block" data-type="blockDistribution"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mob_loot">Mob loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=4&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Mob loot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Mob loot">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Endermen" title="Endermen">Endermen</a> can pick up grass blocks, and drop the blocks they are holding if killed, making it the only way to obtain grass blocks without the use of <a href="/w/Silk_Touch" title="Silk Touch">Silk Touch</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-generation">Post-generation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=5&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Post-generation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Post-generation">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Grass can spread to nearby <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a> blocks, but not <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Coarse_dirt" title="Coarse dirt">coarse dirt</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Rooted_dirt" title="Rooted dirt">rooted dirt</a>. Grass spreading without player intervention depends heavily on the <a href="/w/Daylight_cycle" title="Daylight cycle">time of day</a>.‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup> For a dirt block to accept grass from a nearby grass block, the following requirements must be met:
</p>
<ol><li>The dirt block receiving grass must be within a 3×5×3 range of the source grass block where the source block is in the center of the second topmost layer of that range.</li>
<li>The source grass block must have a <a href="/w/Light" title="Light">light</a> level of 9 or brighter directly above it.‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup></li>
<li>The block directly above the dirt block must allow light to pass through it and hit the dirt block, even though the actual light level does not matter. That means blocks that partially let light through such as stairs and slabs must not have their light-blocking side(s)‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup> facing the dirt block.</li>
<li>The block directly above the dirt block must not be <a href="/w/Lava" title="Lava">lava</a>, <a href="/w/Water" title="Water">water</a>, or a waterlogged variant of a block.</li></ol>
<p>When grass is <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Random_tick" title="Random tick">random ticked</a>, it spreads by checking 4 blocks within range and converts any dirt blocks selected into grass.
</p><p>Though <a href="/w/Water" title="Water">water</a> and <a href="/w/Lava" title="Lava">lava</a> are both <a href="/w/Light#Light-filtering_blocks" title="Light">light-filtering blocks</a> (meaning they decrease skylight by 1 level but do not affect block light), other light-filtering blocks such as <a href="/w/Ice" title="Ice">ice</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Slime_block" title="Slime block">slime blocks</a> do not block grass from spreading to the dirt block. Grass blocks can grow under all other transparent blocks like <a href="/w/Glass" title="Glass">glass</a>, <a href="/w/Fence" title="Fence">fences</a>, or <a href="/w/Torch" title="Torch">torches</a>. Grass jumps directly from one block to a neighbor and is not affected by gaps or other blocks being "in the way." Grass blocks spread at random intervals and have an equal chance of spreading to any suitable dirt blocks that are in range. Because grass can spread as much as 3 levels downward, it tends to spread down slopes much faster than it spreads up them.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=6&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Appearance">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote searchaux" style="font-style: italic; margin-left: 1em;">Main article: <a href="/w/Color#Biome_colors" title="Color">Color § Biome colors</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/w/File:JFgrass.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="854" decoding="async" height="169" loading="lazy" src="/images/thumb/JFgrass.png/300px-JFgrass.png?03e3b" srcset="/images/thumb/JFgrass.png/600px-JFgrass.png?03e3b 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/w/File:JFgrass.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/w/Plains" title="Plains">Plains</a> (left) and <a href="/w/Forest" title="Forest">forest</a> (right) grass colors.</div></div></div>
<p>The coloration of grass blocks is dependent on the <a href="/w/Biome" title="Biome">biome</a> they are in. A grass block always uses the color set to its location, regardless of how it was placed or of its source. This affects the side and top of the block.
</p><p>In <i><a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">Bedrock Edition</a></i>, biome colors also appear on <a href="/w/Map" title="Map">maps</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Color">Color</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=7&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Color">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Color">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Item">Item</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=8&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Item">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Item">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>in <a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>, <span class="sprite-file" style=""><img alt="BlockSprite grass-block.png: Sprite image for grass-block in Minecraft" class="pixel-image" data-file-height="16" data-file-width="16" decoding="async" height="16" loading="lazy" src="/images/BlockSprite_grass-block.png?97c2e" width="16"/></span> item of grass block uses biome color with temperature 0.5, downfall 1.0, and as result is colored <span style="display: inline-block; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="display: inline-block; background-color: #7cbd6b; border: 1px solid #888; border-radius: 0.3em; width: 1em; height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.4em; margin-right: -0.1em"><br/></span> #7cbd6b</span>.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage">Usage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=10&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Usage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Usage">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Using <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Bone_meal" title="Bone meal">bone meal</a> on grass blocks causes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Short_grass" title="Short grass">short grass</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Tall_grass" title="Tall grass">tall grass</a>,‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup> <a href="/w/Fern" title="Fern">ferns</a>,‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Bedrock Edition"><a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">Bedrock Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup> and <a href="/w/Flower" title="Flower">flowers</a> to grow.
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Mobs" title="Mobs">Passive mobs</a> tend to wander toward grass blocks. They also wander toward <a href="/w/Light" title="Light">light</a>.
</p><p>When a <a href="/w/Sheep" title="Sheep">sheep</a> eats a grass block, the block becomes <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a>, and a <a href="/w/Shears" title="Shears">sheared</a> sheep regrows its <a href="/w/Wool" title="Wool">wool</a>. Baby sheep graze grass much more often than adults and mature 1 minute faster when grazing.
</p><p>Tilling a grass block with a <a href="/w/Hoe" title="Hoe">hoe</a> converts it to a <a href="/w/Farmland" title="Farmland">farmland</a> block. 
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Dirt_path" title="Dirt path">Dirt paths</a> can be created by <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.">using</span> any type of <a href="/w/Shovel" title="Shovel">shovel</a> on the side or top of a grass block with air above it. The shovel loses 1 durability for each dirt path block created.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death">Death</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=11&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Death">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Death">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Grass dies and changes to <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a> a random time (when a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Random_tick" title="Random tick">random tick</a> lands on the block) after it has been covered by any <a href="/w/Opacity" title="Opacity">opaque</a> blocks. Transparent blocks can kill grass in a similar manner if they cause the light level above the grass block to be four or below (like water does), and the surrounding area is not otherwise sufficiently illuminated.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spawning">Spawning</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=12&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Spawning">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Spawning">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>, <a href="/w/Mob" title="Mob">animals</a> occasionally <a href="/w/Spawn" title="Spawn">spawn</a> on grass blocks that have light level 9 or brighter in the space directly above. This is quite rare and requires that there be few other animals nearby or in the spawn chunks. Most animals are instead created along with the terrain.
</p><p>In <a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, most animals require surface grass blocks (grass blocks with no solid block anywhere above them at the same x, z coordinate) to spawn. Animals regularly spawn in most Overworld biomes on surface grass blocks that have light level 7 or brighter in the space directly above.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Snowy_grass_block">Snowy grass block</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=13&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Snowy grass block">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Snowy grass block">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/w/File:Snowy_Grass_Block_JE4.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="320" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="160" loading="lazy" src="/images/thumb/Snowy_Grass_Block_JE4.png/150px-Snowy_Grass_Block_JE4.png?35837" srcset="/images/Snowy_Grass_Block_JE4.png?35837 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/w/File:Snowy_Grass_Block_JE4.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A snowy grass block with snow on top of it.</div></div></div>
<p>Grass blocks turn into a snowy grass block if <a href="/w/Snow" title="Snow">snow</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Powder_snow" title="Powder snow">powder snow</a> or a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Snow_block" title="Snow block">snow block</a> is placed on top of the block. Removing the snow layer will turn the block into a normal grass block.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Composting">Composting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=14&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Composting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Composting">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, placing grass blocks into a composter has a 30% chance of raising the compost level by 1.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sounds">Sounds</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=15&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Sounds">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Sounds">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<th>Allowed values</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr><tr><th rowspan="1" style="text-align:left"><b>snowy</b></th><td rowspan="1"><code>false</code></td><td><code>false</code><br/><code>true</code></td><td>If true, the block uses a snowy side and top texture.<br/>In-game, this is true when a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Snow_block" title="Snow block">snow block</a> or <a href="/w/Snow" title="Snow">snow</a> is on top.</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=21&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: History">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable" data-description="History" style="image-rendering: pixelated;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="6"><a href="/w/Java_Edition_pre-Classic" title="Java Edition pre-Classic">Java Edition pre-Classic</a></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="5" rowspan="3"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Cave_game_tech_test" title="Cave game tech test"><i>Cave game tech test</i></a></th><td><a class="image" href="/w/File:Grass_Block_JE1.png"><img alt="Grass Block JE1.png" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="32" loading="lazy" src="/images/thumb/Grass_Block_JE1.png/32px-Grass_Block_JE1.png?46f64" srcset="/images/thumb/Grass_Block_JE1.png/64px-Grass_Block_JE1.png?46f64 2x" width="32"/></a> Added grass blocks.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "''Cave game tech test''",  "content": "(link to File:Grass Block JE1.png article, displayed as 32px) Added grass blocks."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>Grass blocks are one of the first two <a href="/w/Block" title="Block">blocks</a> in <i><a href="/w/Minecraft" title="Minecraft">Minecraft</a></i>, along with <a href="/w/Stone" title="Stone">Stone</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[2]</a></sup>
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "''Cave game tech test''",  "content": "Grass blocks are one of the first two (link to block article, displayed as blocks) in ''(link to Minecraft article, displayed as Minecraft)'', along with (link to Stone article, displayed as Stone)."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>Grass generation is randomized, but it generates only on fully lit tiles. The higher the Y level is, the greater the chance of grass generating. At the top of the map, grass generates on all fully lit tiles.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "''Cave game tech test''",  "content": "Grass generation is randomized, but it generates only on fully lit tiles. The higher the Y level is, the greater the chance of grass generating. At the top of the map, grass generates on all fully lit tiles."}</pre></td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" colspan="5" rowspan="4"><a href="/w/Java_Edition_pre-Classic_rd-20090515" title="Java Edition pre-Classic rd-20090515">rd-20090515</a></th><td><a class="image" href="/w/File:Grass_Block_JE2.png"><img alt="Grass Block JE2.png" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="32" loading="lazy" src="/images/thumb/Grass_Block_JE2.png/32px-Grass_Block_JE2.png?a02d2" srcset="/images/thumb/Grass_Block_JE2.png/64px-Grass_Block_JE2.png?a02d2 2x" width="32"/></a> The top texture and <a href="/w/Model" title="Model">model</a> of grass blocks have been changed.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "rd-20090515",  "content": "(link to File:Grass Block JE2.png article, displayed as 32px) The top texture and (link to model article, displayed as model) of grass blocks have been changed."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>The model now uses new texture on the side faces and <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a> texture on the bottom face.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "rd-20090515",  "content": "The model now uses new texture on the side faces and (link to dirt article, displayed as dirt) texture on the bottom face."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>Grass now spreads to dirt under <a href="/w/Sun#Sunlight" title="Sun">sunlight</a>, allowing new grass blocks to be created.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "rd-20090515",  "content": "Grass now spreads to dirt under (link to Sun#Sunlight article, displayed as sunlight), allowing new grass blocks to be created."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>Due to the lack of dynamic <a href="/w/Light" title="Light">lighting</a> mode, grass in shadows eventually dies and changes to dirt.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java pre-Classic", "version": "rd-20090515",  "content": "Due to the lack of dynamic (link to light article, displayed as lighting) mode, grass in shadows eventually dies and changes to dirt."}</pre></td></tr>

<tr><th colspan="5" rowspan="1"><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210224120652/https://notch.tumblr.com/post/223140045/the-sheep-in-action-considering-making-them-drop" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">October 25, 2009</a></th><td>On <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Notch" title="Notch">Notch</a>'s blog, <a href="/w/Sheep" title="Sheep">sheep</a> were shown to eat grass to regrow wool on their bodies, reverting the block to <a href="/w/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a>. Often, the grass would regrow just as quickly as sheep would eat it.

The only way to kill the grass is to <a href="/w/Breaking" title="Breaking">break</a> the <a href="/w/Block" title="Block">block</a>, so that it <a href="/w/Drops" title="Drops">drops</a> as dirt.

Grass blocks now use grass block top texture on the top face and and dirt texture on the bottom face. The top face is now tinted with <span style="display: inline-block; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="display: inline-block; background-color: #7cbd6b; border: 1px solid #888; border-radius: 0.3em; width: 1em; height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.4em; margin-right: -0.1em"><br/></span> #7cbd6b</span>.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java Beta", "version": "1.8", "snap": "Pre-release 2 ;)", "content": "(link to File:Grass Block (item) JE3.png article, displayed as 32px) The model of grass block in item form have been changed. Grass blocks now use grass block top texture on the top face and and dirt texture on the bottom face. The top face is now tinted with &lt;span style=\"display: inline-block; white-space: nowrap;\"&gt;&lt;span style=\"display: inline-block; background-color: #7cbd6b; border: 1px solid #888; border-radius: 0.3em; width: 1em; height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.4em; margin-right: -0.1em\"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt; #7cbd6b&lt;/span&gt;."}</pre></td></tr><tr><td>Name changed from <i>Grass</i> to <i>Grass Block</i>.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java Beta", "version": "1.8", "snap": "Pre-release 2 ;)", "content": "Name changed from ''Grass'' to ''Grass Block''."}</pre></td></tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Issues">Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=23&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Issues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Issues">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Issues relating to "Grass Block" are maintained on the <a href="/w/Bug_tracker" title="Bug tracker">bug tracker</a>. Report issues <a class="external text" href="https://bugs.mojang.com/issues/?jql=project%20in%20%28MC%2C%20MCPE%29%20and%20%28resolution%20is%20empty%20or%20resolution%20in%20%281%2C%202%2C%206%29%29%20and%20%28summary%20~%20%22Grass%20Block%22%29%20order%20by%20resolution%20desc" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">there</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Grass_Block?section=24&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Trivia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Grass_Block?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Trivia">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Grass blocks and dirt blocks changing between each other is a common cause of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Chunk_updates" title="Chunk updates">chunk updates</a>.</li>
<li>The grass block has become a widely used symbol of <i><a href="/w/Minecraft" title="Minecraft">Minecraft</a></i>.
<ul><li>The icons for <i><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java</a></i> and <i><a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">Bedrock Edition</a></i> apps, except Java snapshots and <a href="/w/Minecraft_Preview" title="Minecraft Preview">Bedrock previews</a>, are based on a grass block.</li>
<li>The favicon for <a href="/w/Minecraft.net" title="Minecraft.net">minecraft.net</a>, as well as the icon for <a href="/w/Minecraft_Launcher" title="Minecraft Launcher">Minecraft Launcher</a>, used to be a grass block.</li></ul></li>
<li>The top face of snowy grass blocks is not affected by biome tinting and therefore appears gray. Normally, snowy grass blocks are covered by snow and their top face cannot be seen by players, unless they create a snowy grass block with no other blocks on its top using commands or the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Debug_stick" title="Debug stick">debug stick</a>.</li></ul>
